Free Talk

A Word of Wisdom 140

— Qiu Shui

▲ Only women request women's suffrage. No man requests to take over a woman's job, willingly staying home to do the cooking. Only women sing loudly about gender equality. No man volunteers to concurrently hold a woman's position. It's evident that women love to meddle in other people's affairs, an undeniable fact.

▲ A modern woman marries the first time out of curiosity, the second time for love, and the third time for money. Considering the facts, none of this is wrong.

▲ The older you get, the heavier the price of love. A young man can love a woman empty-handed. However, once he's over thirty, he needs stacks of banknotes and large diamonds to attract a young woman's heart.

▲ If you understand the possibility of a certain career and put it into practical work, you can achieve success. If you know the limit, you have gained happiness.

▲ A man can pursue a woman tirelessly, but once he gets her, he inevitably yawns.

▲ A woman spends far more time on dressing than the average man. However, nowadays, a man spends far more time on dressing than a woman, because a modern woman's clothes are often five times less than a man's.

▲ A man with a gentle disposition can forgive anyone except a friend who owes him money and a woman who doesn't get along with him.

▲ Anyone likes to give advice to others, but no one likes to listen, and no one can follow it.

▲ General advice is a very well-decorated criticism. Therefore, a person who is good at criticism is good at giving advice.

A Sketch of a Tibetan Youth with Peculiar Talents 141

— Wanderer

The young man's surname is Chen, given name Jichang, a person from a remote area in eastern Tibet. One day, introduced by Mr. Xincun, I met and talked with him several times and came to understand the outline of his drifting and wandering to Shanghai. I hereby record it as follows:

Jichang lost his parents at a young age and had no uncles, brothers, or sisters. He was raised in his maternal family. When he was eight years old, a European named Mr. Lawley came to Tibet, partly to preach and partly to do business. Seeing Jichang, he pitied him and immediately took him back to raise him. Thus, this lonely orphan ascended to a real paradise.

Mr. Lawley was fascinated by science and invented a language machine, spending a research fee of 60,000 pounds and taking more than twenty years to finally succeed. This machine could almost all global languages. Its shape was similar to a phonograph, weighing about forty pounds. It's a pity that Mr. Lawley kept it secret and did not publicize it, so the world didn't know about it.

Jichang was intelligent. From a young age, he was fed when hungry and played when full. In addition to doing some work for Mr. Lawley, he used the language machine to learn languages. He mastered a language every three months. As a result, he was quite fluent in our national language, and he could also recognize some Chinese characters. In addition, he was fluent in thirteen languages, including such as Silturi, English, Australian, Egyptian, Javanese, Indian, Tibetan, Hakka, Xiamen, Shantou, Cantonese, Siamese, and Western dialects. He also followed Mr. Lawley to Europe for four and a half years. Mr. Lawley was also a strange man and didn't tell him about his home. Year after year, he was always on the road. So, when Chen was sixteen, Mr. Lawley suddenly left Chen in Tibet and disappeared. Chen had no choice but to live with his uncle. His uncle was scheming. One day, he sold him to a Mongolian as a slave. Every day he cooked tea, poured urine, and dusted chairs and benches. If he slightly disobeyed the master's wishes, he would be whipped immediately. Jichang couldn't bear the suffering. When the master went to Sichuan to trade, he took Jichang with him. One night, he took the opportunity to run away. He wandered to Shanghai, and his travel expenses were exhausted. He was hungry for three days and slept in the alleys at night. Later, he spoke to an Indian policeman, who pitied him and gave him food and clothing for several days. Later, through the introduction of a certain gentleman, he met Mr. Xincun. Mr. Xincun was compassionate and did his best to help the distressed and relieve the poor. He saw him as different and provided him with food and lodging. He first had him take remedial classes and then planned to find him an opportunity to study. But Chen found it difficult. Mr. Xincun set a self-study schedule for him, requiring him to write a certain amount of large and small characters, read newspapers, read books, and practice English every day, and asked him to do it on time. In the evening, he came from afar to supervise him every day. But Chen's slave nature was deeply rooted, and he was afraid of being lazy. Later, he left. Jichang is eighteen years old. Some people don't think he's Tibetan. In fact, he has a thin, dark face, loves smoking, and doesn't like bathing. He is indeed a Tibetan.

Strange Makeup 142

— Ying Dai

According to news from Los Angeles, USA, green eyebrows, silver eyelashes, and golden yellow ears will soon become new decorations for American girls. This argument was made by Mr. Manson, a hairdresser from the Chicago Beauty Association. According to Manson, it's not just that. From now on, the color painted on American women's fingers will also match the color of their clothes or hair. This dyeing method is quite fast and can be changed at any time, it is said. Wouldn't we consider it a strange talk when we hear about it?

Remembering the Lantern Festival in Yuezhong 143

— Xuehen

The lanterns compete for redness. Suddenly, it's Yue Ren Day. The curtains are rolled up and the wind is gentle. It's the time of the lantern test again. Now is the era of promoting the national calendar. The old lunar lantern festival is like a flower of tomorrow. It should be rare for young people to mention it. But I am a traveler in Shanghai, alone and lonely. Zhong Xuan wrote fu. Jiang Xie recited Yue poems. Thinking of my hometown, how can I stop? I will describe the grand occasion of the lantern festival in Yuezhong in the past to comfort my homesickness. It implies a sense of the changes of the world from the past to the present.

The grandest lantern festivals in Yuezhong are the lantern platforms in Luzhuang and the lantern heads in Taoyan. From the 13th to the 15th night, Jin Wu doesn't prohibit it. The whole city is crazy. The alleys are full of lost slippers. The roads are covered with fallen bracelets. Shoulders rub against each other, and toes touch each other. There is no way to describe its grandeur. The villagers often perform plays during these few days, called lantern head plays. Since there are many plays, you can see stages erected facing each other every ten or tens of steps. The sounds of flutes and pipes are connected to each other. The lanterns include those that resemble people, animals, objects, and flowers and plants, without exception. The lights are strange and dazzling, and cannot be fully understood. In addition to the lantern competition, Luzhuang also has a treasure competition, where the organizers borrow antiques from the local rich families. Antiques, jade, rare treasures, and exotic animals can all be displayed. When I was a child, I heard the old people in the village say that they had seen a coral walking stick that was six or seven feet long and a green jade watermelon. After several changes, I don't know which family these things have flowed into. However, since later generations have been mostly unstable, this custom has gradually declined. I once read the Yuezhong Lantern Poems in the Baihua Jiangfu Pavilion Poetry Collection by the senior Li Chunlao from my hometown. It says: "Good towers on the side of Luzhuang. Ten thousand spring flowers bloom in the candlelight. New makeup comes out to watch under the moon. The fire dragon comes to report the dance in the village ahead." It also says: "The Taoyan Lantern Market is new every year. Everyone celebrates spring together in the temple. The spring stars are gradually scattered and the singing is over. Lanterns help the drunk people in every house." It also says: "What do you do at home to thank the good harvest? I feel even more lost when I think about it as a guest. The first spring night is a good time for the wind and moon. The mountains and rivers are golden and bright for the lantern test day." Closing the book and humming softly, I can't help but deepen my homesickness in this world of red dust.

The First Sound of Butterfly's Voice 144

— Ziwei

Butterfly's performance art has long been recognized as the leading figure in the Chinese film industry. Her slight smile, light frown, slight anger, and other actions, even a gesture or a step, have been deeply imprinted in the minds of our audience. Everything contains the word beauty. But I still feel regret that I can't personally hear her clear singing and charming voice.

Since Western talkies were transported to our country and screened, I have also been to listen and watch. I still feel that the progress of our people is far from as agile as theirs. At that time, I thought that in the near future, there might be domestic works to resist imported goods. Sure enough, as I expected, recently, Mr. Zhang Shichuan, the president of the Mingxing Company, accepted the commission of the Minzhong Company and joined forces with the Pathe Company, which specializes in sound films, and spent six months and cut off 120,000 capital. After four or five trials, the sound was finally tested at the Guanglu Grand Theater. I was fortunate to be invited by a friend to see it first. It turned out that the protagonist of the new film "Songstress Red Peony" was the well-known and famous Ms. Butterfly. When the lady's singing first started, the audience in the hall applauded thunderously. After the movie ended, visitors from all walks of life congratulated the authorities of the Mingxing Company. Everyone said that the ancestor of domestic silent films was "Orphan Saves Ancestor," and the definite arrow of domestic sound films was "Songstress Red Peony." According to the film's beauty, it is tight-knit, can echo back and forth, has a very deep stimulating nature, and can make ordinary female comrades cry out loud. As for the other interlude and supporting roles, they are all the choice of the moment. In my humble opinion, in addition to the hard work of Director Zhang and Ms. Hu, the screenwriter's brain is the most admirable. It is said that the film's release period at sea is imminent, probably to be screened at the Xinguang Grand Theater first.

Small Arts in Wuzhong 145

— Fengmu

Reading the Free Talk, I saw Qing Qu's note about kneading statues in Wuzhong. I still remember this person, and I can remember several things related to him. So, I will write them down together.

(1) Kneading Statues: This person's surname seems to be Xu. At first, he was also a member of the laboring class, not a noble young master. Kneading statues doesn't have to be done at night. Kneading a statue only sells for two Buddha coins. But if you want to make seasonal clothes, hats, shoes, and small shrines for the statue, it will cost dozens to hundreds of yuan, because the cost is huge and it takes a long time. This person has a strange habit. He is never willing to perform his skills for others until the opium is about to run out. This has the air of a famous person. He never taught apprentices, because it was difficult to find someone suitable. He has two sons, neither of whom can pass on his art. So, after his death, no one inherited his industry. What a pity.

(2) Grass Insects Made from Orchid Leaves: Using a single orchid leaf, mantises and grasshoppers are made, all lifelike. When I was a child, I saw them in Yuanmiao Temple. They were sold and made on the spot. The operation was extremely fast. Each one was only sold for three or four coins.

(3) Monkeys Made from Medicinal Herbs: Using a magnolia bud as the monkey's body, a whole cicada skin is disassembled to make the monkey's head and limbs, a thin piece of licorice is used as its crown, and a black bean is used as a peach. Some monkeys squat on rocks, which are sea pumice stones. Each one is also only sold for ten or more coins.

(4) Figures Made from Sweet Potato Flour: Using cooked sweet potato flour, mixed with water of five different colors, various figures and dramas are kneaded, no different from the clay figures in the Yao Huo store under Huiquan Mountain, but more exquisite. The value is determined by the complexity of the process. However, the most expensive ones are not more than a hundred coins. This art was still occasionally seen more than ten years ago, but now it has disappeared, because the cost of living is increasing and those who do this can't make a living, so they all changed to other industries.

(5) Fragrant Beads Carved from Lotus Seeds: The above are all made by people from the lower class. This is made by ladies in wealthy families. The method is to use extremely old lotus seeds, knead them extremely softly by hand, and then carve them with embroidery needles. You can carve whatever you want in the way of calligraphy and painting. But the lotus seeds are easily broken when kneading, and you must use extremely light surgery. It is said that only one or two out of every ten can be made, even for the most skilled surgeons. After eighteen are completed, they are strung with colored silk, and a string of fragrant beads is made. My friend Pan Jun Zhuxiao once had a string, which was handmade by his wife. Everyone who saw it praised it as exquisite.

From this, we know that our Chinese people are most rich in artistic ideas. It is a pity that no one advocates them, letting them disappear without a trace, and even like the Guangling San, which is not passed down to future generations. It is deeply regrettable.

Random Talks on Traveling in Europe (3) 146

— Wang Yachen

At that time, I mentioned the Leifeng Pagoda in West Lake. Its long history can be compared with the Leaning Tower of Pisa. It wasn't until it collapsed suddenly that everyone wanted to rebuild it. It's not necessary to redo historical relics. There are also the sculptures by Yang Hui of Kunshan Yongzhi Town. It wasn't until the broken temple collapsed that everyone sighed. The late Japanese Omura Seigai once told me ten years ago, "If you don't repair it, I am willing to initiate the repair." At that time, I also told many people, but they didn't care about this matter. It's too late to take action after it collapses. Now they are rebuilding the temple, but only four or five of the dozen or so Buddha statues are left. How regrettable this is. But it is also because we lack specialized talents to study antiques.

Seeing an antique can evoke historical, artistic, and emotional influences. The basis of culture lies in this point. I finally feel that it is necessary to organize art galleries in various places in China now. Even if Chinese antiques are transported abroad, there are still many historical heritages that have not been completely moved. Nanjing, Shanghai, and other provinces must organize antique preservation institutions (that is, art galleries). If there is an organization, there will be specialized talents to study it.

The Antique Museum in Beiping has recently been run in a very orderly manner. Tianjin has also successively discovered them. Is it possible that no one cares about this matter in Nanjing, the capital, and Shanghai, the first commercial port in the East? I am determined to promote this matter first after returning to China. People in the country who care about cultural undertakings will also have some sympathy.

An hour after the car departed from Bi Zha, it arrived in Spezia. This question is about beautiful mountains and clear waters. The car circles around the mountains, as if traveling in Switzerland on the mountains. Spezia is surrounded by marble. As seen along the car, the ground is full of marble pieces. Many villagers make a living by opening stones. The car travels about thirty minutes out of the mountain bay, passing through more than twenty mountain tunnels, all along the strait. When passing through the mountain tunnels, it is suddenly bright and dark, making people dizzy. Every time you exit a hole, you can see the sea. After passing through the last mountain tunnel, the station is called Ropallo Station. The buildings along the strait are novel. There are many hotels, like the shores of the Four Forest Lake in Switzerland. It is cleaner than other places. It is said that this is a summer resort. After stopping for twenty minutes, the car continued forward and arrived in Genoa. This is one of the most lively commercial ports in Italy.

Looking far away, there are countless ships parked. The surrounding scenery is excellent. Many passengers got off the car at the R station. After the car left, Yu and Jun stood in the car compartment to dine. Good Italians have guest meals to buy along the way. Various foods are packed in a paper bag, and all the things that should be included in the dinner are fully equipped. Each bag is ten lira (equivalent to two yuan in national currency). The Japanese are good at imitation. The Bian Dang (meals sold at the station) at the station is modeled after this style. The car arrived in Torino in the middle of the night. I transferred to a car going to Lyon, France. After changing cars, there were not many passengers and I rested in the car. I was tired from traveling for several days and slept soundly.

Flour Market Turns Tired After Being Lively 155

Yesterday's flour market, after the opening of each month's market in the morning, once showed a lively image. Although the quotation for foreign wheat rose by about two jiao, and the weather still felt cold since the beginning of spring, yesterday's sixth snowfall also danced, so the hearts of people inside and outside were quite firm. The initial opening of each month was still flat, and then gradually improved, better than the closing of the previous week by more than one point. Until the opening of the afternoon, the situation changed again, and each month fell one after another. The gold price fell sharply, as low as more than 720 taels. The exchange rate had already been extended, and the ordering of foreign wheat became easier. The factories still had a lot of pressure to sell. Later, it was feared that there would be more supply than demand, so it was still seen as tired. As a result, this month was a little bit weaker than the previous day by five li, April and June were unchanged, and May, July, and August were better by two and a half li.

The Futures Wheat Market Goes From Firm to Soft 156

Yesterday's futures wheat market, after the opening in the morning and afternoon, showed a state of initial firmness followed by decline. In the morning, each session quoted foreign wheat due to the cold spring and the sixth snowfall, which was also about two jiao better. Therefore, the thoughts of outsiders turned stronger, and temporary speculative buyers were quite active. The same price of each month had returned to two, three, or four points better. Until the opening in the afternoon, the gold price fell sharply, and the arbitrage of those in the trade was also very smooth. Each month then fell back. Although most of the current settlements are centered on the gold market, in fact, the shorts have foreign wheat in preparation. If the demand is not as strong as the supply, the future will not be stable. As a result, this month was unchanged, April and May were slightly down by one point, June was unchanged, July was better by two points, and August was slightly down by one point.

Northern Traders Slightly Handle Ke Xian Rice 157

Yesterday's Ke Xian rice market conditions remained silent. Only the Qinhuangdao traders in the Tong Market handled 200 bags of Jiangxi Ji Wan rice, and the price was still 13 yuan. In fact, the arrival was hopeless, and the cargo owners were holding on to scarce goods, but the traders did not ask for prices because the price was too high. The market was dull. There were still local customers consulting about Ke Yuan rice, but the arrival was rare and the inventory was scarce. The market will also turn into a state of silence. However, rice merchants will find it difficult to transport Ke Xian rice, and Du rice cannot meet the export demand of Ke rice traders. They will transport rice from Hong Kong, Annam, Siam, and Korea to Shanghai in hopes of meeting the market, but rice from Annam, Siam, etc. cannot make a profit due to the gold price.

The Sugar Market: Taitoo ○ Mark Opens at 2,500 Bags 158

▲ The Trend of Marking Prices is Weak

Yesterday's sugar market reported that the spot sugar price in Cuba remained unchanged, and the New York futures sugar for March also had no rise or fall. Each step of the remaining days fell by one point. Both the existing and futures sugar in Java had no incoming telegrams. In the market of the Public Association, due to the sluggish actual sales and the long foreign exchange rate, the buying interest was even more quiet, and the market situation was weaker. Although Dutch sugar No. 24 refined white sugar was released, it still maintained 10 taels and 7 qian and a half, but the acceptance was quiet, and there were no transactions in the entire market. The trend of Japanese sugar was even more withered, because the factory's selling pressure was very strong. The YT mark price was 10 taels and 6 qian, the YP mark was 10 taels and 8 qian, and the "了" mark was 11 taels. The transactions were very scarce, and the market was flat and tired. Taitoo ○ mark sugar was only allowed to sell half of the delivery in March and April, with a total of 2,500 bags, and the price was 3 yuan and 8 jiao plus tax per day in gold. The price was still appropriate, and Dutch red sugar was affected. The number plates of the state-produced Wufu ice were opened at 100 boxes, and the price was 9 taels, and they were sold through. The stock of Taiyuan ice in the market has been cut off. It is heard that it will arrive in a few days, so the Wufu ice number plate has already been transferred.

Silk and Tea: European and American Silk Telegrams Did Not Turn Around Yesterday 159

Yesterday, the silk market of foreign firms in this port still had no trend of turning smooth. It was found that the overseas silk telegrams did not turn around yesterday, and the exchange rate fluctuated constantly. Although the European firms had a stomach for it, the spot price was not high, and it was difficult for Chinese silk firms to sell. Yesterday, only Hua Tong and other Huaihu white factories processed 20 packages, Ke Chang entered 10 packages of Bai Qian Jing, and Samsung entered 15 packages of coarse silk. The prices were all flat.

Luzhuang Zhenmei Slightly Moves European Sales 160

The selling price of Xia Mu was 41 taels. The selling price of Zhenmei was between 19 taels and 22 taels, and there was no increase or decrease compared with before. Xiumei Gongxi and other items had no transactions in yesterday's market.

Therefore, the Huzhong Pavilion Baize has risen by two and a half li, and Sanyou's return has also risen accordingly, with a selling price of three qian and three fen. Western goods are black soft but white and straight. Bleached cloth Fu 绸 and 生罗 are rising in price. Yuan Yu 绸 has fallen sharply. Shuang Xian 布 has risen sharply. Flannel Sales Rise Sharply 162

法 绒 is a special item needed for making headgear in the western part of Henan, and it is a popular wool product in late spring and early summer. Each of the seagoing woolen goods companies sells it. The average price of the best quality is about five taels per piece, and the second-grade is only sold for two taels. The retail price in the store is different, depending on the quality of the body and the popularity of the market and the sales. Yesterday, the demand for headgear 法 绒 rose sharply. The western clothing tailoring shops of the local traders are all requesting samples and purchasing them. The woolen goods association is also asking each other. The general brand of 法兰 绒 is sold at more than four taels, five taels and two qian and a half, and five taels and five or six qian. The lower grade goods also need to be sold at three taels and a half (formerly only sold at two taels and four or five qian). It is heard that the stock is still lacking and it is difficult to find more.

North and South Goods: Magnolia Seeds Rise Again by Four or Five Taels 163

Because the stock of magnolia seeds is in short supply and the license number has long been cut off, yesterday, Yichang Wheel of Taitoo Company checked and found a batch of only ten boxes imported from Xiamen. The goods were in good condition and were immediately cashed out, which was four or five taels higher than the previous plate. There are still several boxes of secondary merchants that have not been cashed out, but it is still far from the new period. If there are goods with delicate yellow color, the market price may reach 50 taels.

Hardware: English Tinplate Sales Are Smooth 164

The English tinplate market has been exceptionally good recently, presumably because of the small amount of goods and the strong demand. Yesterday, the Xin 泰古 and other repair shops arrived with 2,500 boxes of spot goods. It was found that they were all purchased by the Tianjin traders at a price of 16 taels. Other traders in Kaifeng and Sichuan also want to add more, but there is not much spot goods on the market, so the traders have no goods to purchase. It is heard that foreign firms such as Baolong and Jicheng have spot goods to arrive, so the general purchasers have been contacting them separately, so the market is quite good. The transaction of American goods was still idle yesterday, and the price was 17 taels and a half for 90 pounds and 18 taels and two qian and a half for 100 pounds. It is heard that the transaction was only slightly embellished by the egg factory traders, and there were no other transactions.

Youth Garden

The Bachelor Club of Determined Aspiration 169

— Gou Can

This seems to be a rather peculiar and interesting organization in student life.

Although the co-educational system has been implemented for several years, and the call for gender equality has also attracted the attention of the majority in society, everything in society is always contradictory. In reality, even highly educated ladies seem to be separated by an invisible fence. Among them, female students are often regarded by modern students (?) as special, and they seem to consider it a privilege to get close to them. "Queens," "campus belles," women's photos printed in pictorials, and discussions about female student life in wall newspapers are all products of this. What I am about to say may also be a product of this contradictory society.

On the morning of the fifth, an English notice was suddenly discovered on the bulletin board, with several articles of association attached at the end. Immediately, a group of people gathered around, whispering to each other, their faces showing a kind of surprised expression. It turned out to be a membership recruitment notice for the Bachelor Club (pachojorgclub). Originally, we could also translate it as the "Bachelor Society," but looking at its articles of association, it did not contain a single bachelor's sentiment, but was full of an attitude of seeking love. Under the "Purpose," we can write it as the following: "The purpose of this club is to enhance the goodwill of modern women with a proper attitude and elegant behavior." Under the "Rules," there is the following rule: "All public actions or words between members must be spoken in English in order to maintain confidentiality." In the place where the name is signed, no mailing address is written. Yesterday, someone had already attached the following English sentence to the paper, "Tell me, where is the club address?" But there was no response.

Under the current circumstances, this prominent notice naturally aroused the surprise of the general public, especially among female students. "Who is the initiator, what is the background, what is the purpose?" and similar questions are constantly being asked among the students in search of answers. Therefore, this semi-public, semi-secret notice has become the central point of discussion among the students. Some people think it is a modern act, some people think it is a product of improper motives, some people think it is a manifestation of respect for women, and some people think it is a humiliation of women, and a demon in the call for gender equality. However, although there is constant debate and exploration, no one has yet obtained the answer as to who initiated it, becoming a mystery that all students in the school want to solve.

Dear readers, what kind of environment do you think this is a product of?
